BSKYANGS, GDAN SA'I MKHAN PO SKYABS RJE GSER TOG RIN PO CHES
DBUS MDZAD PA'I DGE 'DUN MANG MA'I SER SPRENG MCHOD ROL

DANG BCAS BLA MA GZHUNG LAS PAS GDUNG DBYANGS DANG BCAS DAR 'BOD
LAN GSUM BYAS NAS PHYAG BTEGS TE THAB BSUR YUD TZAM ROL TE NYIN
GUNG TZAM LA KO KY'A MKHAR GYI NYE 'DEBS SU BZHUGS SGAR STED
PHYAG PHEBS

DE NAS DGONGS JA'I SNGON DU RANG RE'I RI KHROD DU GLO BUR DU
CHIBS BSGYUR BSKYANGS TE LHOD BZHUGS MDZAD, DE NAS YAR BYAMS
KHANG DU CHIBS BSGYUR GNANG NAS RAB GSAL DU SA SROD KYI BAR DU
LHOD BZHUGS MDZAD, DER

GSOL 'O DRANGS, DE NAS MAR BYON TE GZIMS CHUNG DU BZHUGS PAR

TSAD GNYIS BCAS PHUL NAS SKYABS 'JUG ZHU BAR, ^GONG SA MCHOG NAS
SKU

'JUG RI KHROD KYI RTEN SKAL DU BSTZAL, ZHAL NAS RGYA DNGUL RDO
TSAD GNYIS BSTZAL TE RI KHROD 'DIR RJES SU BRGYAD GRVA ZHIG
BTZUGS RGYU SEMS LA BZUNG DE'I THEBS SU YIN GSUNG, SLAR BKA' LAS
SGAR BSGRIGS STENG

DU GSOL DPON MKHAN PO'I KHRIR KHYOD LA GUR THAB GUR GNYIS RGYAB
STE YOD DER BZHUGS RING MDZOD, DE NAS NGED CAG BOD DU LHAN CIG
TU 'GRO ZHES BKA' BSTZAL BA BZHIN DBU GUR STENG DU PHYIR PHEBS
PAS, MUN RUB

DBU GUR STENG DU BYON NO, ,PHYI NYIN STONG 'KHOR MKHAR GYI CO

SKU ZHABS BDE YANGS

KHAR KLU GTOR RAB GNAS SOGS GNANG, SPYIR CHU BO RGYAS PHYIR
DANG, RI KHROD KYI GAM DU CHU MIG RGYAS PA'I SA SOGS GNAS GZIGS
MDZAD, SKU NGAL

BSO STE NYIN GCIG 'JAGS MAL MDZAD, PHYIR PHEBS SKABS RI KHROD DU
PHEBS RGYU'I SNYAN GSAN YANG PHUL, TSES BCO BRGYAD NYIN PHRAN
CAG ZHABS ZHU ZHU STE STONG 'KHOR DU PHUN TSOGS RAB GNAS KYI
KHANG BAR GNAS

'KHOR BCAS DBUS 'GYUR

BRJOD PA NGO TSA BA'I GNAS SU GYUR YOD, LHAG DON KHYAD PAR CAN,
^ GONG SA RGYAL PO'I DBANG PO'I RNAM THAR RGYA MTSO LTA BU LAS
CHU THIGS TZAM ZHIG RANG GZHAN GYI

DAD PA'I GSOS SMAN DU SBEL BAR BYED PA PO NI DGE SBYONG GI SHA
TSUGS CAN CHOS MED BHU SU GU PA ^ CHOS KYI RDO RJES GA-YAR KHRAL
TZAM DU SBEL BA'I RI MO'I LAM DU SPEL BA PO CHOS LA BLO MIG
MCHOG TU YANGS PA DPYOD LDAN DUS GRVA BA DGE SLONG NGAG

DBANG RGYA MTSOS BRIS PA DZA YANTU,, ,,AOm SVA STI, BLOo CHEN
'JAM DPAL SNYING PO'I DGONGS BZANGo BCUD, ,BYANGo CHUBo LAM
BZANG MTSON PA'I MIG GCIG PU, ,BSTANo PA'I YANG SNYING GSAL BYED
SGRONo

ME MCHOG ,RDO RJE 'CHANG DBANG ZHABS RDUL GTZUG TU BSTEN, ,PHUL
BYUNG BSHAD DANG SGRUB PA'I RLABS 'PHRENG GIS, ,NYE BAR BRGYAN
PA'I MDO SNGAGS CHU GTER CHE, ,MKHYEN DPYOD HUB KYIS GSOL TE
MTHA' KLAS 'GROR, ,

STZOL MDZAD THAR LAM STON PA'I SA MKHAN MCHOG ,YAB GCIG 'KHOR
LO'I MGON PO'I GSANG GSUM GYI, ,RLABS CHEN MDZAD BZANG PHA MTHA'
BRAL BA LAS, ,TSUR MTHONG BYIS BLO'I YUL DU GYUR BA RNAMS, ,NYID
KYI

@388B ZHAL KHYIM LAS 'ONGS RTOGS BRJOD 'DI, ,GUS LDAN SKYE BO'I
DAD PA 'PHEL PHYIR DANG, ,RANG GZHAN DGE TSOGS RGYA CHEN SPEL
PA'I SLAD, ,HO CHID MI DBANG GTZO BA'I DAD LDAN RNAMS, ,LHAG
BSAM DAG PAS RGYU YON

LEGS SBYAR TE, ,MI BZAD DPAR DU BSKRUN PA'I DGE TSOGS MTHUS,
,YAB RJE MCHOG GI THUGS DGONGS RDZOGS PA DANG, ,YANG SRID NYIN
BYED GZHON NU MYUR GSAL TE, ,'CHAD RTZOD RTZOM PA'I 'OD SNANG
RTAG 'GYED SHOG  ,

MI DBANG CHAB SRID MNGA' THANG RIGS RGYUD 'PHEL, ,'BREL THOGS
KUN KYANG CHOS MTHUN BSAM DON 'GRUB, ,TSE RABS 'PHRENG BAR RJE
BTZUN BLA MA YI, ,GSUNG GI BDUD RTZIR NGOMS MED LONGS SPYOD SHOG
,KHYAD PAR MA 'ONGS

BYANG PHYOGS K'A LA PAR, ,'KHOR GYI 'DUS PA DANG POR RJES BZUNG
STE, ,SGO GSUM MNYES PA 'BA' ZHIG LHUR BLANGS NAS, ,DANG PO'I
SANGS RGYAS GO 'PHANG MCHOG THOB SHOG , ,,(CES RIGS DANG DKYIL
'KHOR KUN GYI MNGA'

BDAG DRUG PA RDO RJE 'CHANG GSUM LDAN NGUR SMRIG GAR GYI RNAM
PAR ROL BA ^ RJE BTZUN BLA MA DAM PA CHE SHOS MKHAN CHEN RDO RJE
'CHANG CHEN PO DON GYI SLAD DU MTSAN NAS SMOS TE MTSAN BRJOD PAR
DKA' BA ^ RJE BTZUN BLO BZANG BYANG CHUB BSTAN PA'I SGRON ME
DPAL BZANG PO'I

ZHAL SNGA NAS KYI RNAM PAR THAR PA RJE RANG NYID KYIS MDZAD PA
'DI NYID, BSOD NAMS STOBS KYIS MNGON PAR MTHO BA'I SA SKYONG MI
DBANG CHEN PO TZUN HO CHID WANG NAS RGYA SGOR LNGA BRGYA PHUL TE
CIS KYANG PAR DU 'KHOD DGOS TSUL GSUNG NAN CHE BAR BRTEN, GZHAN
YANG

@389A *, ,GSER TOG SGAR BA NAS DNGUL SRANG BCU, AA BHA GA YAN TO
DGON PA'I RDOR SKYABS DKA' BCU NAS GOR MO BRGYA, AA BHA GA DON
YON GNYER BAS GOR MO LNGA BCU, AA BHA GA DGE SLONG CHOS 'KHOR
NAS SGOR MO LNGA, SKU 'BUM DUS 'KHOR GRVA

TSANG NAS GOR MO NYER LNGA, DZA YA SMAN PAS YANG T'A KHA NYER
GCIG ,SGAR GNYER NAS GOR MO BCU BCAS ZHAL 'DEBS SU PHUL BA RNAMS
BSDUS TE, PAR YIG 'BRI MI AA RU HOR CHEN SHOG GI GRVA RIGS DPYOD
LDAN DGE SLONG BLO BZANG DKON MCHOG ,BSGO MKHAN

DPA' RIS DGE TSUL SKAL BZANG SBYIN PA, SGO DMAR MI SKYA BRTZON
'GRUS, RDE'U TSA'I DPON PHAG MO RDO RJE RNAMS KYIS BGYIS TE MJUG
GRUB PAR NYE SKABS, RJE NYID KYI SKU'I GCUNG CHOS MDZOD MKHAN PO
BYAMS SH'AK LAGS NAS LHA RDZAS SRID DU RING BA BDOG PA'I DNGOS
SKYES BCAS PAR BYANG SMON TSIG
